+  <td width=151 style='width:4.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;border-bottom:
+  solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;
+  height:12.1pt'>
+  <p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:8.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
+  style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Make a sound,
+  phone ringtone, notification and loud the conversation sound</span></p>

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc286133272"></a><a
+name="_Toc284061464"></a><a name="_Toc284059550"></a><a name="_Toc283825717"></a><a
+name="_Toc279669531"></a><a name="_Toc279669148"></a><a name="_Toc279656009"></a><a
+name="_Toc279590757"></a><a name="_Toc335987238"></a><a name="_Toc318894036"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893997"></a><a name="_Toc318893964"></a><a name="_Toc318893925"></a><a
+name="_Toc275347803"></a><a name="_Toc182047043"></a><a name="_Toc156377507"></a><a
+name="OLE_LINK33"></a><a name="OLE_LINK32"></a><a name="_Toc467510927"></a><a
+name="_Toc433216651"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>Removing the back cover</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+must remove the back cover to install 4G LTE </span><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>USIM</span><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'> </span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>card, SIM
+card, SD card and Battery. Hold the lower half of the phone with battery cover
+upwards, and lift the bottom of the battery cover, then the battery cover can
+be removed.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=152
+height=103
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image007.jpg"></span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=7 height=7
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; Please turn the phone off before open the
+battery to prevent damage.</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.05pt;text-indent:-9.05pt'><span

+alt=Info> </span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+be careful when opening the back cover, follow it accordingly to prevent damage.</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.05pt;text-indent:-9.05pt'><i><span

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510928"><span lang=EN-US

+the </span></a><span lang=IN style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>USIM</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You must insert<a
+name="OLE_LINK29"></a><a name="OLE_LINK28"> 4G LTE</a> </span><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>USIM</span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'> card is
+on the phone to enjoy and enable all the features</span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>. Your card contains
+all your subscription information.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK2"></a><a
+name="OLE_LINK1"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Insert
+4G LTE </span></a><span lang=IN style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>USIM</span><span

+with the metal contacts facing down and the cut corner is aligned with the
+cutting on the slot.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt'><span

+not installed, or there are errors in the insertion, or the card is damaged,

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510929"></a><a
+name="_Toc335987239"></a><a name="_Toc318894037"></a><a name="_Toc318893998"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893965"></a><a name="_Toc318893926"><span lang=EN-US

+background:#D9D9D9'>nserting SD card</span></h2>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Insert Micro SD card
+with the metal contacts facing down and the cut corner aligned with that of the
+slot</span></p>

+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:16.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span

+when the phone is powered on .the Micro SD-Card or the phone might get damaged
+and the data on the Micro SD-Card could be lost.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span

+width=6 height=6 id="Picture 441"

+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>��</span></i></b><b><i><span

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-align:left;

+font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You might need to restart your phone after
+setting the storage to SD-Card or when inserting an SD-Card.</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=6 height=6 id="Picture 21"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span></i><i><span lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;
+When inserting SD-Card, you will have two options</span></i><i><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>:</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-11.95pt'><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>1.<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></i><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>As internal storage
+&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : Your
+SD Card will have capability like internal memory which can save and install
+application. But, if you choose this menu you should format your SD Card and
+your existing data will be lost. </span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-11.95pt'><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>2.<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></i><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>As portable
+storage&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; :
+Your SD Card can only be used as multimedia data storage, such as: photos,
+videos, songs and documents.</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-align:left;
+text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><a
+name="_Toc335987242"></a><a name="_Toc318894040"></a><a name="_Toc318894001"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893968"></a><a name="_Toc318893929"></a><a name="_Toc275347806"><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510930"></a><a
+name="_Toc433216654"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>Installing the battery</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You must install and
+charge the battery to use your phone. Insert the ridge at the top of the
+battery into the base of the phone, make sure to touch the metal contact on the
+phone, then push the battery down and snap it into place.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=7 height=7
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; Do not forces to turn the phone back on
+over and over if the battery is too low, it might cause damage to the phone and
+the battery.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-align:left;
+text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=7 height=7 id="ͼƬ 29"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; Please turn the phone off before open the
+battery</span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>
+</span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>to
+prevent damage</span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><b><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#CCCCCC'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><b><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Note:</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Your phone is
+designed to be used only with the original batteries and chargers. The use of
+other battery or charger is not recommended it may cause damage to your phone
+and the warranty will be void.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-autospace:none'><a
+name="_Toc335987241"></a><a name="_Toc318894039"></a><a name="_Toc318894000"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893967"></a><a name="_Toc318893928"></a><a name="_Toc275347805"><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:18.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=140 height=81 id="ͼƬ 17"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image013.jpg"></span></b></a></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510931"></a><a
+name="_Toc433216655"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>Removing the battery</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Make sure your phone
+is powered off before taking out the battery to prevent data loss from the
+phone. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=131
+height=84 id="ͼƬ 16"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image014.jpg"></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:18.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510932"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Charging
+the battery</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>New batteries are
+shipped partially charged. Before you can use your phone, you need to charge
+the battery. Some batteries will have best performance after several full
+charge/discharge cycles, follow the instruction bellow:</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Connect
+data cable and charger, plug one end into your phone��s data port.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Plug
+the other end of the charger into the appropriate electrical outlet (100~240V
+AC).</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>When
+your phone indicates that the battery is fully charged, remove the charger.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:14.2pt;layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:14.2pt;text-indent:-14.2pt;text-autospace:
+none'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Notes:</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+battery is removable, please properly install them to prevent damage, and use
+the original battery and charger</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK30"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Your phone
+is designed to be used only with original batteries and chargers</span></i></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+battery can discharge gradually even when your phone is powered off. If the
+battery is drained for a long time, the information stored in the phone could
+possibly be lost. </span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Even when
+you are not using the phone, it would be best to charge your phone periodically
+to keep it away from draining.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK23"></a><a name="OLE_LINK22"></a><a
+name="OLE_LINK3"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If the
+battery is charged after draining, the phone cannot be turned on. The battery
+needs to be charged for a while, afterward then the phone will go to power-off
+charging mode and you can turned on the </span></i></a><i><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>phone</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK5"></a><a name="OLE_LINK4"><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You need
+longer charging period with the lower voltage.</span></i></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Recommendations
+do not operate phone during charging.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+normal temperature of charging is during 0&#8304;C- 40&#8304;C.<a name="_Toc335987243"></a><a
+name="_Toc318894041"></a><a name="_Toc318894002"></a><a name="_Toc318893969"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893930"></a><a name="_Toc275347808"></a></span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510934"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Basic
+Operations</span></a></h2>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510935"></a><a
+name="_Toc335987245"></a><a name="_Toc275347810"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Turning
+on and off the phone</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><a
+name="OLE_LINK9"></a><a name="OLE_LINK8"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
+6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To turn on the phone: </span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Press
+Power key for more than 3 seconds to turn on your phone. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To turn off the
+phone: </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Press Power key to
+pop up option menu, select ��power off��. If it is powered off you cannot receive,
+make a call or do other operations.<a name="_Toc335987246"></a></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510936"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Get
+Started</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><b><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Set up your phone</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The<span
+style='color:black;letter-spacing:.55pt'> first time you turn on the phone,
+you'll see a Welcome screen.</span></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>&Oslash;<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To choose a
+different language, touch the Start.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>&Oslash;<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To set up your
+phone, touch the Start and follow the instruction, such as select a SIM for
+cellular/calls/test messages etc. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>&Oslash;<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You need to connect
+to an active network or WI-FI to proceed.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK27"></a><a
+name="OLE_LINK26"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>There
+will be series of screens takes you through the setup </span></a><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>process. Set
+up complete, click ��GOT IT�� to enter home screen.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;<img width=62
+height=110 id="ͼƬ 0"

+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US

+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc335987248"></a><a

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510937"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Making

+name="OLE_LINK35"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Making

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:1.15pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Touch</span><span

+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>. If you
+make a mistake, you can touch</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;

+all numbers before the cursor.</span><span lang=IN style='font-size:6.0pt;
+font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'> Touch</span><span lang=EN-US

+width=14 height=13
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image022.png"></span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>to make a
+</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>voice
+</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>call</span><span

+as you desired.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:1.15pt;margin-bottom:
+0cm;margin-left:14.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-9.65pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:black;

+SIM1 network only.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:1.15pt;margin-bottom:
+0cm;margin-left:14.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-9.65pt;text-autospace:
+none'><a name="OLE_LINK25"></a><a name="OLE_LINK24"><span lang=EN-US

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510939"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#CCCCCC'>Optimize

+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:1.15pt'><span lang=IN style='font-size:
+6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You&nbsp;can&nbsp;extend&nbsp;your&nbsp;battery's
+&nbsp;between&nbsp;charges by turning off features that you don't need. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:1.15pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>First touch the Settings
+icon</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>
+<b><img width=13 height=13 id="ͼƬ 176"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image034.png"></b>&nbsp;on
+a Home or All Apps screen.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><b><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Extend&nbsp;the&nbsp;life&nbsp;of&nbsp;your&nbsp;battery</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'>If you&nbsp;aren't&nbsp;using&nbsp;Wi-Fi,
+Bluetooth, or GPS, use the Settings app to turn them off: <b>Settings </b></span><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>��</span></b><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'> </span></b><b><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt'>Location</span></b><b><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt'> or Wi-fi or Bluetooth</span></b><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt'>.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'>Turn&nbsp;off&nbsp;GPS:&nbsp;Touch&nbsp;<b>Settingsl&nbsp;</b></span><b><span

+6.0pt'>then&nbsp;switch&nbsp;off&nbsp;the&nbsp;Location.&nbsp;</span></p>

+<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'>Turn&nbsp;down&nbsp;screen&nbsp;brightness&nbsp;and&nbsp;set&nbsp;a&nbsp;shorter
+Sleep timeout:</span><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'> Settings </span></b><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>��</span></b><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'> </span></b><b><span lang=EN-US

+<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

+text-justify:inter-ideograph'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'>Note that&nbsp;this&nbsp;means&nbsp;you&nbsp;need&nbsp;to&nbsp;sync&nbsp;manually

+<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;

+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

+<p class=MsoNormalCxSpFirst style='text-autospace:none'><b><span lang=EN-US

+<p class=MsoNormal><a name="OLE_LINK46"></a><a name="OLE_LINK43"><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Send and
+receive message.</span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Create
+text message</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Touch
+<img width=16 height=15 id="ͼƬ 9"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image049.png">&nbsp;<b>Messaging
+</b>icon to open the program.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Click
+<img width=14 height=13 id="ͼƬ 6"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image050.png">&nbsp;to
+create message.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Input
+receiver��s phone number and edit contents.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>For
+phone number:</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+can click the keyboard to input number directly.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+can select number from messages, contacts or groups</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+can select several numbers to send.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>4.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+color:black;letter-spacing:.35pt'>Touch<img width=16 height=13 id="ͼƬ 51"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image051.png">to
+send the message by LTE/SIM1 network.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>5.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
+6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";font-weight:normal'>Touch</span></span><span
+class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+font-weight:normal'> </span></span><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;
+font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=14 height=13 id="ͼƬ 19"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image052.png"></span></b><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b><span
+class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+font-weight:normal'>and </span></span><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
+6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=16 height=13 id="ͼƬ 54"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image053.png"></span></b><span
+class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+font-weight:normal'>&nbsp;to send the message by SIM2 network.</span></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=7 height=7 id="Picture 73"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp; Mes</span></i><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>sage with
+attachment, Multimedia Message (MMS) are not supported</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:7.1pt;text-indent:-7.1pt'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Notes:</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If the
+message editing is interrupted by incoming calls, alarm clock, powering off,
+the entered texts will be saved temporarily. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Click
+��Type message�� to edit the message.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Touch
+<img width=6 height=13 id="ͼƬ 12"
+src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image054.png">&nbsp;button
+to show the menu.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Message
+with attachment are not supported features.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><a
+name="_Toc318894050"></a><a name="_Toc318894011"></a><a name="_Toc318893978"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893939"><span lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=1151><a name="_Toc467510945"></a><a name="_Toc335987276"></a><a
+name="_Toc327173404"></a><a name="_Toc272851842"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt'>Safety and Use</span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+read carefully and observe the following regulations to avoid damaging your
+telephone or using it against the law.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Electronic
+devices/Health care facilities.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Turn
+off your phone when you are near high-precision electronic devices in use to
+avoid causing malfunction or interfering with their operation (fire alarms,
+automatic doors and automatic control equipment).</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Turn
+off your phone in hospitals or places where the use of mobile phones is
+restricted. Mobile phones affect the normal operation of electronic devices and
+medical instruments, such as pacemakers, hearing aids and other electronic
+medical devices.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Pacemaker
+manufacturers recommend that mobile phones are kept at least 15 cm away from
+pacemakers to prevent the phone interference. When using the phone, you should
+hold it against the ear on the opposite side to the device, to reduce
+interference.&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Mobile
+phones should be forbidden inside an operating theatre, Intensive Care Unit
+(ICU) or Cardiac Care Unit (CCU). </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Pay
+attention to the settings of the sound volume and the vibration to avoid
+disturbing the patients.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Flammable
+or explosive areas</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Turn
+off your phone near flammable or explosive areas. Do not install/remove or
+charge the battery or use the phone in these areas to prevent any explosion or
+fire. Flammable and explosive areas include: chemical plants, facilities with
+chemical substances or particles in the air (grains, dust and metal powder ),
+petrol stations and fuel depots, fuel storage areas (for example, under a
+ship��s deck), areas with explosion warning signs, areas with ��turn off two-way
+radio equipment�� signs and places where you are usually recommended to switch
+off car engines. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b><span lang=EN-GB
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Safety
+of use in a vehicle</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+observe the relevant local or national regulations related to the use of mobile
+phones in a vehicle. Please refrain from using the phone while driving. If you
+are driving and need to use the phone in an emergency, use a hands-free device
+(optional purchase) to be safe. Otherwise, park the car before using the phone.
+</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place your phone on the dashboard or within an airbag deployment area to
+avoid causing injury to passengers in the car when the bag inflates or bursts. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Using
+the phone on an airplane is strictly forbidden. Turn off your phone before you
+board an aircraft. It is recommended to remove the battery to avoid the phone
+being turned on accidentally.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Storing
+environment</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To
+avoid demagnetizing problem, keep the phone away from magnetic materials, such
+as magnetic discs and credit cards.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Ensure
+that the phone does not come into contact with liquids. If it does, turn it off
+immediately, remove the battery and quickly contact the vendor.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not store the phone, battery or charger in an environment with a strong
+magnetic field, such as an electromagnetic pot or a microwave oven, to avoid
+causing the phone to malfunction, catch fire or explode. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not subject the phone, battery or charger to heavy impact or vibration to avoid
+battery leakage, phone malfunction, overheating, fire or explosion</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place sharp metallic items such as needles, near the receiver because the
+receiver will attract them and you may be injured when using the phone.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place the phone in the back pocket of your trousers or skirt to avoid
+damaging it when you sit down</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Child
+health</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Keep
+the phone, battery and charger out of the reach of children. Do not let
+children use the phone, battery or charger without supervision.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not let a child put a battery in his/her mouth to avoid electrolyte poisoning.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Keep
+children away from small phone accessories to prevent suffocation or blocking
+of the oesophagus as a result of swallowing.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Operating
+environment</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>This
+phone is equipped with a built-in antenna. When the phone is on, unless
+necessary, do not touch the antenna area (top of the phone) for optimal
+communication quality.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not use your phone while it is being charged during thunderstorms, or use it
+outdoors to avoid being struck by lightning or other injury.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not use your mobile phone in dusty, wet, dirty places or places near magnetic
+fields to prevent malfunction of its internal circuits. Keep the phone as dry
+as possible. Keep the phone, battery and charger away from water and water
+vapour and do not clean the phone with a wet cloth to avoid short circuits,
+malfunction due to corrosion and electric shocks.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not turn in or off the phone against your ear to avoid your ears and body from
+being impaired.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To
+comply with regulations on radio frequency exposure, keep the antenna at least
+one inch (2.5 cm) away from your body when holding your phone or using its data
+functions.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+you feel unwell (epileptic seizures or blackouts) after playing the games with
+your phone for a long period of time, please seek medical assistance
+immediately.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Move
+your mobile phone away from your ear while using the hands-free mode, because
+the amplified volume might cause hearing damage.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Make
+sure you switched off your phone in areas where mobile phone use is prohibited!</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Cleaning
+and maintenance</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Switch
+off the phone before cleaning and maintenance. The charger should be unplugged
+from the power socket and the phone and charger disconnected to prevent any
+electric shock or short circuiting of the battery or charger.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not wipe the phone or charger using chemical substance (alcohol benzene),
+chemical agents or abrasive cleaning agents to avoid damaging its parts or
+causing a malfunction. You may clean with a slightly damp anti-static soft
+cloth.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not scrape or alter the phone case as paint substances may cause an allergic
+reaction. If such a reaction occurs, cease using the phone immediately and seek
+medical help.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Wipe
+dust off the power plug and keep it dry to avoid risk of fire</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the phone or accessories do not work properly, contact your local vendor</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not dismantle the phone or its accessories yourself.<br>
+<br>
+</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Protecting
+the environment</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+observe the local regulations on phone packaging, battery and used phone
+disposal and bring them to the collection point for proper recycling. Do not
+dispose of used phones or batteries in a household rubbish bin.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+take your used, unwanted lithium batteries to a designated place. Do not
+dispose of them in a rubbish bin.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal>
+
+<table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 align=left>
+ <tr>
+  <td width=3 height=0></td>
+ </tr>
+ <tr>
+  <td></td>
+  <td><img width=73 height=35
+  src="user_manual_indonesia.files/image055.png"
+  alt=Hong></td>
+ </tr>
+</table>
+
+<br clear=ALL>
+</p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Emergency
+call</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>In
+an emergency situation, if the phone is on and you are within the network
+range, it can be used to make an emergency call. However, emergency call
+numbers may not be reachable on all networks; you should never rely on your
+mobile phone for emergency calls.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Using
+the battery and charger </span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Only
+use batteries and chargers approved by the manufacturer. Do not use batteries
+or chargers that are not compatible with your model to avoid any explosion. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not throw a battery in a fire as it might catch fire or explode. Do not cause a
+short circuit to the charger as it might result in malfunction, smoke or
+fire.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place conductors like metals, keys or jewels, against the battery poles or
+allow them to touch the ends of the battery to avoid short circuiting the
+battery and causing injury (burns, for example) as a result of battery
+overheating </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the power cable is damaged (wires exposed or broken) or the connection to the
+plug is loose, do not use it to avoid electric shock, short-circuit of the
+charger or a fire.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not dismantle the battery or weld the two poles of the battery to prevent the
+battery from leaking, overheating, catching fire or exploding. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Keep
+the charger away from any container of water or other liquids. Infiltration of
+liquid may cause electric leakage or other malfunction to the charger.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the battery leaks, emits smoke or a strange odour, cease use immediately and
+move it far away from naked flames or people to avoid a fire or injury from
+explosion. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not charge the battery in a dusty or damp environment and keep the cable away
+from heated objects. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+battery is not fully charged when leaving the factory. Therefore, you should
+charge the battery for two hours before use. Before charging, make sure the
+charge plug is correctly inserted in the power socket. If it is incorrectly
+inserted, electric shock might occur and the phone or battery may catch fire or
+explode. When charging is completed, pull out the charger plug from the power
+socket, and do not pull the cable.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the liquid in the battery splashes into your eyes, do not rub the eyes to avoid
+damaging your vision, rinse the eyes immediately in clean water and go to a
+hospital for assistance.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place heavy objects on the charger cable. Do not damage, twist or pull the
+cable to avoid causing electric shock or fire.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>When
+the battery cannot be installed correctly in the phone, do not press down on it
+heavily to prevent it from leaking or exploding. Do not remove the battery when
+the phone is on. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the battery is distorted, has changed colour or is unusually hot when charging
+or when it is stored, remove immediately the battery and stop using it or it
+may leak, become overheated, explode or catch fire. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+a battery is not used for a long period of time after charging, store it at
+room temperature</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not touch the power socket, power cable or charger with wet hands to avoid
+electric shock.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+water or other liquid enters the charger, immediately disconnect the charger
+plug from the power socket to prevent it from overheating, catching a fire or
+malfunction.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Explanation:</span></b><span
+lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'> The
+instructions in this user manual apply to English mode. In other language
+operating modes, slight differences may appear.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Warning:
+</span></b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+manufacturer disclaims any liability for damage, which may result as a
+consequence of improper use of this mobile phone or use contrary to the
+instructions contained in this manual.<a name="_Toc335987277"></a></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc286133272"></a><a
+name="_Toc284061464"></a><a name="_Toc284059550"></a><a name="_Toc283825717"></a><a
+name="_Toc279669531"></a><a name="_Toc279669148"></a><a name="_Toc279656009"></a><a
+name="_Toc279590757"></a><a name="_Toc335987238"></a><a name="_Toc318894036"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893997"></a><a name="_Toc318893964"></a><a name="_Toc318893925"></a><a
+name="_Toc275347803"></a><a name="_Toc182047043"></a><a name="_Toc156377507"></a><a
+name="OLE_LINK33"></a><a name="OLE_LINK32"></a><a name="_Toc467510927"></a><a
+name="_Toc433216651"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>Removing the back cover</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+must remove the back cover to install 4G LTE </span><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>USIM</span><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'> </span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>card, SIM
+card, SD card and Battery. Hold the lower half of the phone with battery cover
+upwards, and lift the bottom of the battery cover, then the battery cover can
+be removed.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:8.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=152
+height=103
+src="user_manual.files/image007.jpg"></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=7 height=7
+src="user_manual.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; Please turn the phone off before open the
+battery to prevent damage.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.05pt;text-indent:-9.05pt'><span
+lang=EN-US><img width=7 height=7 id="Picture 433"
+src="user_manual.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info> </span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+be careful when opening the back cover, follow it accordingly to prevent damage.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.05pt;text-indent:-9.05pt'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510928"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Inserting
+the </span></a><span lang=IN style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>USIM</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;
+font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'> and SIM Card</span></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You must insert<a

+on the phone to enjoy and enable all the features</span><span lang=EN-US

+all your subscription information.</span></p>

+name="OLE_LINK1"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Insert

+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'> and SIM card
+with the metal contacts facing down and the cut corner is aligned with the

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510929"></a><a

+background:#D9D9D9'>nserting SD card</span></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Insert Micro SD card
+with the metal contacts facing down and the cut corner aligned with that of the
+slot</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US

+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;text-autospace:none'><b><span

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span

+when the phone is powered on .the Micro SD-Card or the phone might get damaged

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span

+setting the storage to SD-Card or when inserting an SD-Card.</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img

+When inserting SD-Card, you will have two options</span></i><i><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>:</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-11.95pt'><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>1.<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></i><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>As internal storage
+&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; : Your
+SD Card will have capability like internal memory which can save and install
+application. But, if you choose this menu you should format your SD Card and
+your existing data will be lost. </span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.3pt;text-indent:-11.95pt'><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>2.<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></i><i><span
+lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>As portable
+storage&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; :
+Your SD Card can only be used as multimedia data storage, such as: photos,
+videos, songs and documents.</span></i></p>

+text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span

+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510930"></a><a
+name="_Toc433216654"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>Installing the battery</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You must install and
+charge the battery to use your phone. Insert the ridge at the top of the
+battery into the base of the phone, make sure to touch the metal contact on the
+phone, then push the battery down and snap it into place.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=7 height=7
+src="user_manual.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; Do not forces to turn the phone back on
+over and over if the battery is too low, it might cause damage to the phone and
+the battery.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='margin-left:9.35pt;text-align:left;
+text-indent:-9.35pt'><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=7 height=7 id="ͼƬ 29"
+src="user_manual.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:

+battery</span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>
+</span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>to
+prevent damage</span></i><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>.</span></i></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><b><span lang=EN-US

+

+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Note:</span></b></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Your phone is

+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510931"></a><a
+name="_Toc433216655"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+background:#D9D9D9'>Removing the battery</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Make sure your phone
+is powered off before taking out the battery to prevent data loss from the
+phone. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=131
+height=84 id="ͼƬ 16"
+src="user_manual.files/image014.jpg"></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:18.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span lang=IN
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510932"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Charging
+the battery</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>New batteries are
+shipped partially charged. Before you can use your phone, you need to charge
+the battery. Some batteries will have best performance after several full
+charge/discharge cycles, follow the instruction bellow:</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Connect
+data cable and charger, plug one end into your phone��s data port.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Plug
+the other end of the charger into the appropriate electrical outlet (100~240V
+AC).</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>When
+your phone indicates that the battery is fully charged, remove the charger.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:14.2pt;layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:14.2pt;text-indent:-14.2pt;text-autospace:
+none'><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Notes:</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+battery is removable, please properly install them to prevent damage, and use
+the original battery and charger</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK30"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Your phone
+is designed to be used only with original batteries and chargers</span></i></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+battery can discharge gradually even when your phone is powered off. If the
+battery is drained for a long time, the information stored in the phone could
+possibly be lost. </span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Even when
+you are not using the phone, it would be best to charge your phone periodically
+to keep it away from draining.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK23"></a><a name="OLE_LINK22"></a><a
+name="OLE_LINK3"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If the
+battery is charged after draining, the phone cannot be turned on. The battery
+needs to be charged for a while, afterward then the phone will go to power-off
+charging mode and you can turned on the </span></i></a><i><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>phone</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK5"></a><a name="OLE_LINK4"><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You need
+longer charging period with the lower voltage.</span></i></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:
+"Arial","sans-serif"'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Recommendations
+do not operate phone during charging.</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510934"><span lang=EN-US

+Operations</span></a></h2>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510935"></a><a
+name="_Toc335987245"></a><a name="_Toc275347810"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Turning
+on and off the phone</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><a
+name="OLE_LINK9"></a><a name="OLE_LINK8"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
+6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To turn on the phone: </span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Press
+Power key for more than 3 seconds to turn on your phone. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To turn off the
+phone: </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Press Power key to
+pop up option menu, select ��power off��. If it is powered off you cannot receive,
+make a call or do other operations.<a name="_Toc335987246"></a></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="_Toc467510936"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Get
+Started</span></a></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><b><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Set up your phone</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The<span
+style='color:black;letter-spacing:.55pt'> first time you turn on the phone,
+you'll see a Welcome screen.</span></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>&Oslash;<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To choose a
+different language, touch the Start.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>&Oslash;<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To set up your
+phone, touch the Start and follow the instruction, such as select a SIM for
+cellular/calls/test messages etc. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;text-autospace:
+none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Wingdings'>&Oslash;<span
+style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'> </span></span><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You need to connect
+to an active network or WI-FI to proceed.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><a name="OLE_LINK27"></a><a
+name="OLE_LINK26"><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>There
+will be series of screens takes you through the setup </span></a><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>process. Set
+up complete, click ��GOT IT�� to enter home screen.</span></p>

+<p class=MsoNormal style='text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US

+<h2 style='layout-grid-mode:char'><a name="OLE_LINK45"></a><a name="OLE_LINK44"></a><a

+
+<p class=MsoNormal><a name="OLE_LINK46"></a><a name="OLE_LINK43"><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Send and
+receive message.</span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Create
+text message</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Touch
+<img width=16 height=15 id="ͼƬ 9"
+src="user_manual.files/image049.png">&nbsp;<b>Messaging
+</b>icon to open the program.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Click
+<img width=14 height=13 id="ͼƬ 6"
+src="user_manual.files/image050.png">&nbsp;to
+create message.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Input
+receiver��s phone number and edit contents.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>For
+phone number:</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+can click the keyboard to input number directly.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+can select number from messages, contacts or groups</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>You
+can select several numbers to send.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>4.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+color:black;letter-spacing:.35pt'>Touch<img width=16 height=13 id="ͼƬ 51"
+src="user_manual.files/image051.png">to
+send the message by LTE/SIM1 network.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt;layout-grid-mode:
+char;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:
+"Calibri","sans-serif"'>5.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
+6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";font-weight:normal'>Touch</span></span><span
+class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+font-weight:normal'> </span></span><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;
+font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=14 height=13 id="ͼƬ 19"
+src="user_manual.files/image052.png"></span></b><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b><span
+class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+font-weight:normal'>and </span></span><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
+6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img width=16 height=13 id="ͼƬ 54"
+src="user_manual.files/image053.png"></span></b><span
+class=Arial2CharChar><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";
+font-weight:normal'>&nbsp;to send the message by SIM2 network.</span></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'><img
+width=7 height=7 id="Picture 73"
+src="user_manual.files/image012.png"
+alt=Info></span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp; Mes</span></i><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>sage with
+attachment, Multimedia Message (MMS) are not supported</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:7.1pt;text-indent:-7.1pt'><i><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><b><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Notes:</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='layout-grid-mode:char;text-autospace:none'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If the
+message editing is interrupted by incoming calls, alarm clock, powering off,
+the entered texts will be saved temporarily. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span

+��Type message�� to edit the message.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Touch
