+to show the menu.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Message
+with attachment are not supported features.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><a
+name="_Toc318894050"></a><a name="_Toc318894011"></a><a name="_Toc318893978"></a><a
+name="_Toc318893939"><span lang=IN style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt;text-indent:-9.0pt'><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=1151><a name="_Toc467510945"></a><a name="_Toc335987276"></a><a
+name="_Toc327173404"></a><a name="_Toc272851842"><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt'>Safety and Use</span></a></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+read carefully and observe the following regulations to avoid damaging your
+telephone or using it against the law.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Electronic
+devices/Health care facilities.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Turn
+off your phone when you are near high-precision electronic devices in use to
+avoid causing malfunction or interfering with their operation (fire alarms,
+automatic doors and automatic control equipment).</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Turn
+off your phone in hospitals or places where the use of mobile phones is
+restricted. Mobile phones affect the normal operation of electronic devices and
+medical instruments, such as pacemakers, hearing aids and other electronic
+medical devices.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Pacemaker
+manufacturers recommend that mobile phones are kept at least 15 cm away from
+pacemakers to prevent the phone interference. When using the phone, you should
+hold it against the ear on the opposite side to the device, to reduce
+interference.&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Mobile
+phones should be forbidden inside an operating theatre, Intensive Care Unit
+(ICU) or Cardiac Care Unit (CCU). </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Pay
+attention to the settings of the sound volume and the vibration to avoid
+disturbing the patients.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Flammable
+or explosive areas</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Turn
+off your phone near flammable or explosive areas. Do not install/remove or
+charge the battery or use the phone in these areas to prevent any explosion or
+fire. Flammable and explosive areas include: chemical plants, facilities with
+chemical substances or particles in the air (grains, dust and metal powder ),
+petrol stations and fuel depots, fuel storage areas (for example, under a
+ship��s deck), areas with explosion warning signs, areas with ��turn off two-way
+radio equipment�� signs and places where you are usually recommended to switch
+off car engines. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b><span lang=EN-GB
+style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Safety
+of use in a vehicle</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+observe the relevant local or national regulations related to the use of mobile
+phones in a vehicle. Please refrain from using the phone while driving. If you
+are driving and need to use the phone in an emergency, use a hands-free device
+(optional purchase) to be safe. Otherwise, park the car before using the phone.
+</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place your phone on the dashboard or within an airbag deployment area to
+avoid causing injury to passengers in the car when the bag inflates or bursts. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Using
+the phone on an airplane is strictly forbidden. Turn off your phone before you
+board an aircraft. It is recommended to remove the battery to avoid the phone
+being turned on accidentally.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Storing
+environment</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To
+avoid demagnetizing problem, keep the phone away from magnetic materials, such
+as magnetic discs and credit cards.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Ensure
+that the phone does not come into contact with liquids. If it does, turn it off
+immediately, remove the battery and quickly contact the vendor.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not store the phone, battery or charger in an environment with a strong
+magnetic field, such as an electromagnetic pot or a microwave oven, to avoid
+causing the phone to malfunction, catch fire or explode. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not subject the phone, battery or charger to heavy impact or vibration to avoid
+battery leakage, phone malfunction, overheating, fire or explosion</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place sharp metallic items such as needles, near the receiver because the
+receiver will attract them and you may be injured when using the phone.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place the phone in the back pocket of your trousers or skirt to avoid
+damaging it when you sit down</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Child
+health</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Keep
+the phone, battery and charger out of the reach of children. Do not let
+children use the phone, battery or charger without supervision.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not let a child put a battery in his/her mouth to avoid electrolyte poisoning.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Keep
+children away from small phone accessories to prevent suffocation or blocking
+of the oesophagus as a result of swallowing.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Operating
+environment</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>This
+phone is equipped with a built-in antenna. When the phone is on, unless
+necessary, do not touch the antenna area (top of the phone) for optimal
+communication quality.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not use your phone while it is being charged during thunderstorms, or use it
+outdoors to avoid being struck by lightning or other injury.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not use your mobile phone in dusty, wet, dirty places or places near magnetic
+fields to prevent malfunction of its internal circuits. Keep the phone as dry
+as possible. Keep the phone, battery and charger away from water and water
+vapour and do not clean the phone with a wet cloth to avoid short circuits,
+malfunction due to corrosion and electric shocks.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not turn in or off the phone against your ear to avoid your ears and body from
+being impaired.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>To
+comply with regulations on radio frequency exposure, keep the antenna at least
+one inch (2.5 cm) away from your body when holding your phone or using its data
+functions.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+you feel unwell (epileptic seizures or blackouts) after playing the games with
+your phone for a long period of time, please seek medical assistance
+immediately.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Move
+your mobile phone away from your ear while using the hands-free mode, because
+the amplified volume might cause hearing damage.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Make
+sure you switched off your phone in areas where mobile phone use is prohibited!</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Cleaning
+and maintenance</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Switch
+off the phone before cleaning and maintenance. The charger should be unplugged
+from the power socket and the phone and charger disconnected to prevent any
+electric shock or short circuiting of the battery or charger.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not wipe the phone or charger using chemical substance (alcohol benzene),
+chemical agents or abrasive cleaning agents to avoid damaging its parts or
+causing a malfunction. You may clean with a slightly damp anti-static soft
+cloth.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not scrape or alter the phone case as paint substances may cause an allergic
+reaction. If such a reaction occurs, cease using the phone immediately and seek
+medical help.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Wipe
+dust off the power plug and keep it dry to avoid risk of fire</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the phone or accessories do not work properly, contact your local vendor</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not dismantle the phone or its accessories yourself.<br>
+<br>
+</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Protecting
+the environment</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+observe the local regulations on phone packaging, battery and used phone
+disposal and bring them to the collection point for proper recycling. Do not
+dispose of used phones or batteries in a household rubbish bin.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Please
+take your used, unwanted lithium batteries to a designated place. Do not
+dispose of them in a rubbish bin.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal>
+
+<table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 align=left>
+ <tr>
+  <td width=3 height=0></td>
+ </tr>
+ <tr>
+  <td></td>
+  <td><img width=73 height=35
+  src="user_manual.files/image055.png"
+  alt=Hong></td>
+ </tr>
+</table>
+
+<br clear=ALL>
+</p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Emergency
+call</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>In
+an emergency situation, if the phone is on and you are within the network
+range, it can be used to make an emergency call. However, emergency call
+numbers may not be reachable on all networks; you should never rely on your
+mobile phone for emergency calls.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Using
+the battery and charger </span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Only
+use batteries and chargers approved by the manufacturer. Do not use batteries
+or chargers that are not compatible with your model to avoid any explosion. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not throw a battery in a fire as it might catch fire or explode. Do not cause a
+short circuit to the charger as it might result in malfunction, smoke or
+fire.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place conductors like metals, keys or jewels, against the battery poles or
+allow them to touch the ends of the battery to avoid short circuiting the
+battery and causing injury (burns, for example) as a result of battery
+overheating </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the power cable is damaged (wires exposed or broken) or the connection to the
+plug is loose, do not use it to avoid electric shock, short-circuit of the
+charger or a fire.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not dismantle the battery or weld the two poles of the battery to prevent the
+battery from leaking, overheating, catching fire or exploding. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Keep
+the charger away from any container of water or other liquids. Infiltration of
+liquid may cause electric leakage or other malfunction to the charger.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the battery leaks, emits smoke or a strange odour, cease use immediately and
+move it far away from naked flames or people to avoid a fire or injury from
+explosion. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not charge the battery in a dusty or damp environment and keep the cable away
+from heated objects. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+battery is not fully charged when leaving the factory. Therefore, you should
+charge the battery for two hours before use. Before charging, make sure the
+charge plug is correctly inserted in the power socket. If it is incorrectly
+inserted, electric shock might occur and the phone or battery may catch fire or
+explode. When charging is completed, pull out the charger plug from the power
+socket, and do not pull the cable.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the liquid in the battery splashes into your eyes, do not rub the eyes to avoid
+damaging your vision, rinse the eyes immediately in clean water and go to a
+hospital for assistance.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not place heavy objects on the charger cable. Do not damage, twist or pull the
+cable to avoid causing electric shock or fire.&nbsp; </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>When
+the battery cannot be installed correctly in the phone, do not press down on it
+heavily to prevent it from leaking or exploding. Do not remove the battery when
+the phone is on. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+the battery is distorted, has changed colour or is unusually hot when charging
+or when it is stored, remove immediately the battery and stop using it or it
+may leak, become overheated, explode or catch fire. </span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+a battery is not used for a long period of time after charging, store it at
+room temperature</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Do
+not touch the power socket, power cable or charger with wet hands to avoid
+electric shock.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>If
+water or other liquid enters the charger, immediately disconnect the charger
+plug from the power socket to prevent it from overheating, catching a fire or
+malfunction.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></b></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Explanation:</span></b><span
+lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'> The
+instructions in this user manual apply to English mode. In other language
+operating modes, slight differences may appear.</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>Warning:
+</span></b><span lang=EN-GB style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>The
+manufacturer disclaims any liability for damage, which may result as a
+consequence of improper use of this mobile phone or use contrary to the
+instructions contained in this manual.<a name="_Toc335987277"></a></span></p>
+
+<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:5.0pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif"'>&nbsp;</span></p>
+
+<h2><a name="_Toc467510946"></a><a name="_Disclaimer"></a><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.5pt;font-family:"Calibri","sans-serif";background:#D9D9D9'>Disclaimer</span></h2>
+
+<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;
+margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:9.05pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;
+text-justify:inter-ideograph;text-indent:-9.05pt'><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>��<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
+</span></span><span class=hps><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'>The
+usage of non-original accessories such a</span></span><span class=hps><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman","serif"'>s </span></span><span
+class=hps><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'>headsets</span></span><span
+lang=EN-US style='font-size:6.0pt'>, </span><span class=hps><span lang=EN-US
+style='font-size:6.0pt'>batteries, chargers etc, will cause i</span></span><span

+        android:persistent="true"

+            android:label="@string/activity_name"
+            android:icon="@drawable/ic_settings_user_manual" >

+                <action android:name="com.android.settings.action.EXTRA_SETTINGS"/>

Index: vendor/sprd/platform/packages/apps/UserManual/src/com/android/user/manual/UserManualActivity.java
===================================================================
--- vendor/sprd/platform/packages/apps/UserManual/src/com/android/user/manual/UserManualActivity.java	(revision 0)
+++ vendor/sprd/platform/packages/apps/UserManual/src/com/android/user/manual/UserManualActivity.java	(revision 172485)
@@ -0,0 +1,38 @@
+package com.android.user.manual;
+
+import android.app.Activity;
+import android.os.Bundle;
+import android.webkit.WebView;
+import android.webkit.WebViewClient;
+import android.webkit.CookieManager;
+import android.util.Log;
+import java.util.Locale;
+
+public final class UserManualActivity extends Activity {
+    public static final String TAG = "UserManualActivity";
+    @Override
+    protected void onCreate(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
+        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState);
+        setContentView(R.layout.user_manual);
+        WebView webView = (WebView) findViewById(R.id.webview);
+        CookieManager.setAcceptFileSchemeCookies(true);
+        webView.getSettings().setJavaScriptEnabled(true);
+
+        webView.setWebViewClient(new WebViewClient() {
+                @Override
+                public boolean shouldOverrideUrlLoading(WebView webView, String url) {
+                    return false;
+                }
+        });
+
+        final Locale currentLocale = Locale.getDefault();
+        String lan = currentLocale.getLanguage();
+        if ("in".equals(lan)) {
+            Log.d(TAG, "Indonesia");
+            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/user_manual_indonesia.htm");
+        } else {
+            Log.d(TAG, "Others");
+            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/user_manual.htm");
+        }
+    }
+}
Index: vendor/sprd/platform/packages/apps/UserManual/res/values-zh-rCN/strings.xml
